                InInventory WitchavenClass { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, ChickenKillCount, 70, 162; }

                InInventory RRClass { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, ChickenKillCount, 70, 162; }

                InInventory Hexen2Class { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, ChickenKillCount, 70, 146; }
            } else {
                GameMode Deathmatch, Possession, TeamGame
                {
                    InInventory not StrifeClass {
                    InInventory not WitchavenClass {
                    InInventory not RRClass {
                    InInventory not Hexen2Class
                    {
                        DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, Frags, 70, 170;
                    }}}}

                    InInventory StrifeClass { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, Frags, 70, 162; }

                    InInventory RRClass { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, Frags, 70, 162; }

                }

                GameMode SinglePlayer, Cooperative, Invasion, Survival
                {
                    InInventory not StrifeClass {
                    InInventory not WitchavenClass {
                    InInventory not RRClass {
                    InInventory not Hexen2Class
                    {
                        DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, KillCountAmountTrue, 70, 170;
                    }}}}

                    InInventory StrifeClass { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, KillCountAmountTrue, 70, 162; }

                    InInventory WitchavenClass { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, KillCountAmountTrue, 70, 162; }

                    InInventory RRClass { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, KillCountAmountTrue, 70, 162; }

                    InInventory Hexen2Class { DrawNumber 4, INDEXFON, White, KillCountAmountTrue, 70, 146; }
                }
            }

            // Keys
            GameMode SinglePlayer, Cooperative, Invasion, Survival
            {
                InInventory CatacombClass { DrawKeyBar 100, Horizontal, ReverseRows, 10, 221, 148, 0, 14, 12; }
                else { DrawKeyBar 100, Horizontal, ReverseRows, 10, 221, 156, 0, 14, 12; }
            }

            // Mugshot
            //DrawMugShot 5, 73, 168;

            // Inventory
            DrawSelectedInventory AlwaysShowCounter, HUDFONT_DOOM, 290, 22, 293, 30, Untranslated;

            InInventory WolfenClass
            {
                InInventory WolfenClassMode, 2 {} // Totenkopf
                else

                    {
                        InInventory WolfenClassMode, 1 { DrawImage "WLF2LIFE", 290, 48; } // Lost
                        else { DrawImage "WOLFLIFE", 290, 48; } // Classic

                        DrawNumber 10, HUDFONT_DOOM, Untranslated, WolfExtraLife, 293, 56;
                    }
                }
            }

            InInventory DukeClass
            {
                InInventory DukeJetpackFuel { DrawNumber 3, INDEXFON, Yellow, DukeJetpackFuel, 293, 48; }
                InInventory DukeVisionFuel

                    else { DrawNumber 3, INDEXFON, Green, DukeVisionFuel, 293, 48; }

            InInventory KatarnClass

        }
